</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>DERIVATIVE ACTION </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I><U>The United States District Court for the Northern District of</U> </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I><U>California, San Francisco Division, authorized</U><U> this Notice.</U> </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I><U>This is not a solicitation from a lawyer.</U> </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">TO: ALL PERSONS AND ENTITIES WHO CURRENTLY OWN ALPHABET INC. COMMON STOCK </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>PLEASE</B> <B>READ</B> <B>THIS</B> <B>NOTICE</B> <B>CAREFULLY</B> <B>AND</B> <B>IN</B> <B>ITS</B> <B>ENTIRETY</B>. This Notice relates to a
proposed settlement (&#147;<B>Settlement</B>&#148;) of the following derivative action: <I>In</I> <I>re</I> <I>Alphabet</I> <I>Inc</I>., <I>Shareholder</I> <I>Derivative</I> <I>Litigation</I>, Consolidated Case No. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3:21-cv-09388-RFL</FONT></FONT></FONT> (the &#147;<B>Action</B>&#148;). Your rights will be affected by the proposed Settlement.<B> </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All capitalized terms used in this Notice that are not otherwise defined herein have the meanings provided in the Stipulation and Agreement of
Settlement entered into on May&nbsp;30, 2025 (&#147;<B>Stipulation</B>&#148;), by and among (1)&nbsp;Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit and Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System (collectively, the &#147;<B><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs</B>&#148;); (2) Nominal Defendant Alphabet Inc. (&#147;<B>Alphabet</B>&#148; or the &#147;<B>Company</B>&#148;); and (3)&nbsp;Larry Page, Sergey Brin, John L. Hennessy, L. John Doerr, K. Ram
Shriram, Ann Mather, Allan R. Mulally, Roger W. Ferguson, Jr., Robin L. Washington, Frances H. Arnold, Sundar Pichai, and Eric E. Schmidt (collectively, the &#147;<B>Individual Defendants</B>&#148; and, together with Alphabet,
&#147;<B>Defendants</B>,&#148; and, together with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs, the &#147;<B>Settling</B> <B>Parties</B>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>THIS</B> <B>NOTICE</B> <B>PROVIDES</B> <B>ONLY</B> <B>A</B> <B>SUMMARY</B> <B>OF</B> <B>THE</B> <B>MATERIAL</B> <B>TERMS</B> <B>OF THE</B>
<B>SETTLEMENT</B> <B>AND</B> <B>RELEASES</B>. You can obtain more information by reviewing the Stipulation, which is available on Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s website at<BR>
<U>https://scott-scott.com/sdsettlements/alphabet-derivative-settlement/</U>, and on Alphabet&#146;s investor relations website at <U>https://abc.xyz/investor/</U>. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">DERIVATIVE ACTION </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">CASE NO.
3:21-<SMALL>CV</SMALL><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">-09388-RFL</FONT> </P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Because the Settlement involves the resolution of a derivative action, which was brought on
behalf of and for the benefit of the Company, the benefits from the Settlement will go to Alphabet. Individual Alphabet stockholders will not receive any direct payment from the Settlement. <B>ACCORDINGLY</B>, <B>THERE</B> <B>IS</B> <B>NO</B>
<B>PROOF</B> <B>OF</B> <B>CLAIM</B> <B>FORM</B> <B>FOR</B> <B>STOCKHOLDERS</B> <B>TO SUBMIT</B> <B>IN</B> <B>CONNECTION</B> <B>WITH</B> <B>THIS</B> <B>SETTLEMENT</B>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHAT IS THE PURPOSE OF THIS NOTICE? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1. The purpose of this Notice is to explain the Action, the terms of the proposed Settlement of those litigations, and how the proposed
Settlement affects Alphabet stockholders&#146; legal rights. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. The United States District Court for the Northern District of California,
San Francisco Division (the &#147;<B>Court</B>&#148;) will hold a hearing (&#147;<B>Settlement</B> <B>Hearing</B>&#148;) on September 30, 2025, at 1:30 p.m., both in person at the San Francisco Courthouse of the United States District Court for the
Northern District of California, Courtroom 15, 18th Floor, 450 Golden Gate Ave., San Francisco, CA 94102, and online via the Court&#146;s public hearing Zoom Webinar&#151;accessible at
<U>https://cand-uscourts.zoomgov.com/j/1615482105?pwd=cTZiSVdXelllSXpjQ1p0Nm5HaXRYUT09</U>, Webinar ID: 161 548 2105 and password: 315725, at which the Court will consider whether the Judgment, substantially in the form of Exhibit D to the
Stipulation, should be entered: (a)&nbsp;approving the terms of the Settlement as fair, reasonable, and adequate, and in the best interests of Alphabet and Alphabet&#146;s stockholders; (b)&nbsp;dismissing with prejudice the Action pursuant to the
terms of this Stipulation; and (c)&nbsp;ruling upon Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s application for a Fee and Expense Award; and (d)&nbsp;to consider any other matters that may properly be brought before the Court in connection with the
Settlement. The Settlement Hearing date may be subject to change by the Court without any further notice to the class, i.e., Alphabet stockholders. Please check Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s website at
<U>https://scott-scott.com/sdsettlements/alphabet-derivative-settlement/</U>, Alphabet&#146;s investor relations website at <U>https://abc.xyz/investor/</U>, or the Court&#146;s PACER website at
<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://ecf.cand.uscourts.gov/cgi-bin/DktRpt.pl?388891</FONT></U> to confirm that the date has not changed. To access PACER, you must have a user ID and password, which you can obtain via
<U>https://pacer.uscourts.gov/register-account/pacer-case-search-only</U>. Alternatively, please <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-mail</FONT> Patrick Coughlin, Scott+Scott Attorneys at Law LLP, at pcoughlin@scott-scott.com and he shall help
provide you copies of filings in this case that you request. You may also access the case docket in person by going to the Clerk&#146;s Office at the U.S. District Court for the Northern District of California, 450 Golden Gate Ave., San Francisco,
CA 94102. The Court also has instructions for accessing court documents at: <U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://cand.uscourts.gov/about/clerks-office/obtaining-copies-of-court-documents/</FONT></FONT></U>.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHAT IS THIS CASE ABOUT? WHAT HAS HAPPENED SO FAR? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">THE FOLLOWING DESCRIPTION OF THE ACTION AND THE SETTLEMENT HAS BEEN PREPARED BY COUNSEL FOR THE SETTLING PARTIES. THE COURT HAS MADE NO FINDINGS WITH RESPECT
TO SUCH MATTERS, AND THIS NOTICE IS NOT AN EXPRESSION OR STATEMENT BY THE COURT OF FINDINGS OF FACT. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1
</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND
PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF DERIVATIVE ACTION </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>A.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Factual Background </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3. The Settlement arises out of the Action, which alleged breaches of fiduciary duties, among other claims, against certain officers and
directors of the Company. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs alleged in their Litigations that the Individual Defendants breached their fiduciary duties by exposing the Company to antitrust investigations and enforcement
actions by the Department of Justice and state attorneys general, as well as other related civil litigation. Among other things, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs alleged that Alphabet&#146;s Board of Directors (the
&#147;<B>Board</B>&#148;) and certain Company&#146;s senior executives and former executives, failed to properly oversee or caused the Company to pursue anticompetitive business practices, exposing the Company to the risk of liability under U.S.
antitrust law in connection with the Company&#146;s search, Ad Tech, and Android mobile operating system and app distribution businesses. Defendants deny all allegations made by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs in the
Action. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>B.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>The Federal Litigation </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">4. The Settlement arises out of the Action, which alleged breaches of fiduciary duties, among other claims, against certain officers and
directors of the Company. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs alleged in their Litigations that the Individual Defendants breached their fiduciary duties by exposing the Company to antitrust investigations and enforcement
actions by the Department of Justice and state attorneys general, as well as other related civil litigation. Among other things, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs alleged that Alphabet&#146;s Board of Directors (the
&#147;<B>Board</B>&#148;) and certain Company&#146;s senior executives and former executives, failed to properly oversee or caused the Company to pursue anticompetitive business practices, exposing the Company to the risk of liability under U.S.
antitrust law in connection with the Company&#146;s search, Ad Tech, and Android mobile operating system and app distribution businesses. Defendants deny all allegations made by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs in the
Action. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">5. On December&nbsp;3, 2021, Plaintiff Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit filed a shareholder derivative
action in the United States District Court for the Northern District of California, San Jose Division, against Defendants (<I>Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit v. Page</I>, Case No. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5:21-cv-09388).</FONT></FONT> The same day, Plaintiff Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System separately filed a shareholder derivative action in the same court against Defendants (<I>Bucks County Employees&#146;
Retirement System</I> <I>v. Page</I>, Case No. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">5:21-cv-09389).</FONT></FONT> Prior to filing suit, Plaintiff Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit and Plaintiff
Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System propounded shareholder inspection demands on Alphabet and had received productions of books and records from Alphabet. Relevant portions of those productions were included in Plaintiff Police and Fire
Retirement System of the City of Detroit and Plaintiff Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System&#146;s complaints, which were filed under seal. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">6. On December&nbsp;6, 2021, Plaintiff Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit and Plaintiff Bucks County Employees&#146;
Retirement System filed a joint stipulation and proposed order with the Court to consolidate the <I>Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit </I>and <I>Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System</I> actions, appoint themselves as
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-lead</FONT> plaintiffs, and appoint Scott+Scott Attorneys at Law LLP as lead counsel. On December&nbsp;8, 2021, the Court ordered that the <I>Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit </I>and
<I>Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System</I> actions be consolidated, appointed Plaintiff Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit and Plaintiff Bucks County Employees&#146; Retirement System as <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs, and appointed Scott+Scott Attorneys at Law LLP as Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel. On December&nbsp;16, 2021, the Court ordered a joint stipulation directing
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs to file a consolidated complaint. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2
</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND
PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF DERIVATIVE ACTION </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">7. On January&nbsp;14, 2022, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs
filed a consolidated complaint in the Litigation asserting five claims: (1)&nbsp;breach of fiduciary duty against the Individual Defendants in their capacity as directors; (2)&nbsp;breach of fiduciary duty against Defendants Brin, Page, Schmidt, and
Pichai in their capacity as officers; (3)&nbsp;breach of fiduciary duty against Defendants Brin, Page, and Schmidt in their capacity as controlling shareholders; (4)&nbsp;unjust enrichment; and (5)&nbsp;corporate waste (<I>In re Alphabet, Inc.
Shareholder Derivative Litigation</I>, Case No. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3:21-cv-09388-RLF,</FONT></FONT></FONT> ECF No.&nbsp;32, the &#147;<B>Consolidated
Complaint</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">8. On April&nbsp;15, 2022, the Settling Parties filed a stipulation and proposed order to temporarily stay the
Litigation for six months, extendable by agreement of the Settling Parties, pending developments in the antitrust lawsuits underlying the allegations in the Consolidated Complaint. The Court granted the stay later on April&nbsp;15, 2022. By
agreement of the Settling Parties, the stay was extended to January&nbsp;15, 2023. At the Court&#146;s direction, the Settling Parties filed a Joint Status Report under seal on February&nbsp;16, 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">9. The Court then held a Case Management Conference on April&nbsp;20, 2023, at which the Court continued the stay and ordered a further Case
Management Conference set for October&nbsp;19, 2023. Following a joint stipulation by the Settling Parties, the Court continued the Case Management Conference to November&nbsp;2, 2023. On November&nbsp;2, 2023, the Court ordered a further Case
Management Conference on February&nbsp;15, 2024. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">10. On November&nbsp;27, 2023, the Litigation was reassigned to the Honorable Judge Rita
F. Lin in the San Francisco Division. The Court vacated all case management conference dates. Pursuant to orders by the Court, the Settling Parties submitted Joint Case Management Statements on December&nbsp;11, 2023, June&nbsp;12, 2024, and
December&nbsp;12, 2024, each providing the Court an update on the underlying antitrust litigations involving Alphabet. The Court ordered continuations of the stay in the Litigation on December&nbsp;26, 2023, June&nbsp;12, 2024, and December&nbsp;13,
2024. On March&nbsp;5, 2025, the Settling Parties filed a Stipulation and Proposed Order to continue the stay until May&nbsp;30, 2025, which the Court ordered on March&nbsp;6, 2025.&#8195; </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>C.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>The State Action </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">11. On June&nbsp;16, 2022, Plaintiff Jamie Komen Revocable Trust filed a shareholder derivative lawsuit in Superior Court of the State of
California, County of Santa Clara (<I>Jamie Komen Revocable Trust v. Page</I>, Case No. 22CV399340, the &#147;<B>State Action</B>&#148; in the &#147;<B>State Court</B>&#148;) against the Individual Defendants, Does 1&#150;25, and Alphabet. The State
Action brought claims for: (1)&nbsp;breach of fiduciary duty; (2)&nbsp;unjust enrichment; and (3)&nbsp;indemnification and contribution. On June&nbsp;21, 2022, the State Court deemed the State Action a complex action and ordered a stay of discovery
and responsive pleadings. The State Court set the initial Case Management Conference for October&nbsp;27, 2022. Pursuant to stipulations by the parties to the State Action on October&nbsp;13, 2022, January&nbsp;19, 2023, May 4, 2023,
November&nbsp;6, 2023, December&nbsp;8, 2023, March&nbsp;18, 2024, April&nbsp;12, 2024, June&nbsp;20, 2024, September&nbsp;6, 2024, December&nbsp;3, 2024, January&nbsp;31, 2025, and March&nbsp;27, 2025, the State Court continued the initial Case
Management Conference in the State Action pending further developments in the underlying antitrust litigations involving Alphabet. On March&nbsp;28, 2025, the State Court continued the initial Case Management Conference to June&nbsp;12, 2025. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3
</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND
PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF DERIVATIVE ACTION </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>D.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>The Mediations and Extensive Settlement Negotiations </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">12. Prior to filing the <I>Police and Fire Retirement System of the City of Detroit </I>and <I>Bucks</I> <I>County Employees&#146; Retirement
System</I> actions, Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel reviewed internal documents produced by Alphabet in response to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs&#146; shareholder inspection demands. These documents included, among other
things, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(1)&nbsp;non-privileged</FONT> Board materials relating to antitrust investigations or litigations involving Alphabet and the U.S. Department of Justice, Office of the Attorney General of Texas, Office of the
Attorney General of Colorado, or U.S. House Committee on the Judiciary; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(2)&nbsp;non-privileged</FONT> Board materials produced to the foregoing government entities in connection with any investigations of Alphabet
for allegations of anticompetitive conduct; and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(3)&nbsp;non-privileged</FONT> Board materials relating to any U.S. civil litigation by nongovernmental litigants concerning antitrust or anticompetitive conduct
allegations. On May&nbsp;31, 2022, Alphabet further produced to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs documents that were produced by Google to the Texas Attorney General in connection with that office&#146;s investigation of
Google&#146;s business practices, consisting of 133,000 documents totaling 1,117,604 pages. These documents were produced to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs under mediation privilege to assist in the evaluation of their
claims and the mediation process. On June&nbsp;9, 2023, Alphabet produced transcripts of depositions and associated exhibits in certain underlying antitrust lawsuits to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs for use in the
ongoing mediation process. On November&nbsp;1, 2024, Alphabet further produced 52,818 pages of trial exhibits from the antitrust lawsuits underlying the allegations in the Consolidated Complaint. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">13. The Settling Parties have engaged in multiple <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediations under the guidance of the
Honorable Layn R. Phillips (Ret.), formerly the Chief Judge of the United States District Court for the Western District of Oklahoma. The first <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">full-day</FONT> mediation session occurred <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> on December&nbsp;15, 2022, and included participation by Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel, Defendants&#146; Counsel, and a representative from Alphabet. The Settling Parties and a representative from Alphabet
participated in a second <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">full-day</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediation on February&nbsp;7, 2024. The Settling Parties and a representative from Alphabet participated in a third <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">full-day</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediation on September&nbsp;27, 2024, at which the Settling Parties engaged in further discussions of the merits of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs&#146; claims and the Settling Parties&#146; proposals for corporate reforms. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">14. Throughout and following the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediations, Judge Phillips continued to facilitate
discussions between the Settling Parties, the merits of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs&#146; claims, and the potential for settlement. Following extensive negotiations through Judge Phillips, the Settling Parties
requested the issuance of a mediator&#146;s proposal concerning the amount of the proposed compliance spend commitment on February&nbsp;28, 2025, which the Settling Parties accepted, subject to approvals, on March&nbsp;5, 2025. The accepted
mediator&#146;s proposal included all substantive terms of the settlement, including the corporate reforms and compliance spend commitment by Alphabet. Following agreement on these terms, and with the assistance of Judge Phillips, the Settling
Parties agreed to the terms set out in Section V.1, which set out all substantive terms of the proposed settlement on March&nbsp;13, 2025. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">15. After agreeing to all substantive terms of the proposed settlement, subject only to management/Board approval, Judge Phillips facilitated
negotiations between the Settling Parties concerning the amount of any Fee and Expense Award. The Settling Parties requested a mediator&#146;s proposal concerning any Fee and Expense Award on March&nbsp;25, 2025, which the Settling Parties accepted
on March&nbsp;31, 2025. Following acceptance of the mediator&#146;s proposal, the Settling Parties executed the Memorandum of Understanding on April&nbsp;9, 2025. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4
</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND
PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF DERIVATIVE ACTION </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">16. The Settling Parties entered into the Stipulation on May&nbsp;30, 2025. Prior to signing
the Stipulation, the Settling Parties had no negotiations regarding the amount of any Fee and Expense Awards or the amount of any Service Awards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">17. On July 8, 2025, the Court entered the Preliminary Approval Order in connection with the Settlement which, among other things,
preliminarily approved the Settlement, authorized this Notice to be provided to current Alphabet stockholders, and scheduled the Settlement Hearing to consider whether to grant final approval of the Settlement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHAT ARE THE TERMS OF THE SETTLEMENT? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">18. In consideration of the Settlement and the releases provided therein, and subject to the terms and conditions of this Stipulation, the
Settling Parties have agreed to the following Settlement Consideration for Alphabet. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">19. <U>Regulatory Readiness Compliance
Enhancements.</U> Alphabet shall adopt and/or maintain (to the extent already implemented) the corporate governance and workplace measures and enhancements set forth in Paragraph 1.2 of the Stipulation. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">20. <U>Board Oversight Enhancements.</U> The Board shall create a new Risk and Compliance Committee (&#147;RCC&#148;) of the Board. The
substantive terms of the RCC are described in Paragraph 1.4 of the Stipulation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">21. <U>Management Oversight Enhancements.</U> The Company
will maintain a management to assist the RCC to oversee and monitor the Company&#146;s compliance with regard to Google LLC (including its subsidiaries), as outlined in Paragraph 1.5 of the Stipulation. The Company will also maintain a management
steering committee to support the management council as described in Paragraph 1.5 of the Stipulation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">22. To provide funding for its
cross-company global compliance initiatives, Alphabet shall cause to be spent at least $500&nbsp;million over the course of up to 10 years following the Effective Date of the Settlement on its global compliance efforts. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">23. The Company will also maintain the Google Chat policy, process, and/or technical capabilities described in Paragraph 1.7 of the
Stipulation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHAT ARE THE SETTLING PARTIES&#146; REASONS FOR THE SETTLEMENT? </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>E.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Why did the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs agree to settle?
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">24. As discussed above, Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have reviewed and analyzed voluminous confidential, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-public</FONT> internal documents. In addition, Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have reviewed and analyzed data from many other sources specific to this matter, including, but not limited to: (1)&nbsp;Alphabet&#146;s
public filings with the SEC, press releases, announcements, transcripts of investor conference calls, and news articles; (2)&nbsp;securities analyst, business, and financial media reports about Alphabet; (3)&nbsp;internal Alphabet documents produced
pursuant to mediation privilege; (4)&nbsp;deposition </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5
</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND
PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF DERIVATIVE ACTION </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">transcripts and exhibits and trial exhibits in the underlying antitrust lawsuits produced pursuant to
mediation privilege; and (5)&nbsp;trial transcripts and pleadings from the underlying antitrust lawsuits. Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have also (1)&nbsp;researched the applicable law with respect to the claims asserted (or which could be asserted)
in the stockholder derivative actions and the potential defenses thereto; (2)&nbsp;researched, drafted, and filed complaints or sent inspection demands; (3)&nbsp;consulted with experts retained on numerous matters relevant to the pending litigation
and settlement issues; (4)&nbsp;prepared detailed mediation statements; (5)&nbsp;reviewed documents and information provided in advance of the mediation sessions and during settlement negotiations; (6)&nbsp;participated in multiple <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">in-person</FONT> mediations; and (7)&nbsp;engaged in months-long settlement discussions with Defendants&#146; counsel. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">25. Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel believe that the claims asserted in the Litigation have merit and that their investigation of the evidence
supports the claims asserted. Without conceding the merit of any of the Defendants&#146; defenses, and in light of the benefits of the Settlement as well as to avoid the potentially protracted time, expense, and uncertainty associated with continued
litigation, including potential trial(s) and appeal(s), <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs and Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have concluded that it is desirable that the Litigation be fully and finally settled in the manner
and upon the terms and conditions set forth in this Stipulation. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs and Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel recognize the significant risk, expense, and length of continued proceedings necessary to
prosecute the Litigation against Defendants through trial(s) and through possible appeal(s). Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have also taken into account the uncertain outcome and the risk of any litigation, especially complex litigation such as the
Litigation, the difficulties and delays inherent in such litigation, the cost to Alphabet&#151;on behalf of which <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs filed the Litigation&#151;and distraction to management of Alphabet that
would result from extended litigation. Based on their evaluation, and in light of what Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel believe to be the significant benefits conferred upon Alphabet as a result of the Settlement,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs and Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have determined that the Settlement is in the best interests of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs and Alphabet and have agreed to
settle the Litigation upon the terms and subject to the conditions set forth herein. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>F.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B>Why did the Settling Defendants and the Company agree to settle? </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">26. Each Individual Defendant has denied and continues to deny that he or she has committed or attempted to commit any violations of law, any
breaches of fiduciary duty owed to Alphabet, or any wrongdoing whatsoever, and expressly maintains, that at all relevant times, he or she acted in good faith and in a manner that he or she reasonably believed to be in the best interests of Alphabet
and its stockholders. Defendants further deny that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs, Alphabet, or its stockholders suffered any damage or were harmed as a result of any act, omission, or conduct by the Individual
Defendants as alleged in the Litigation or otherwise. Defendants further assert, among other things, that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs lack standing to litigate derivatively on behalf of Alphabet because the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs have not yet pleaded, and cannot properly plead, that a demand on the Board would be futile. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">27. Alphabet nonetheless believes that the Settlement is in the best interests of the Company, its stockholders, and its employees. Defendants
are, therefore, entering into this Settlement for its benefits and to eliminate the uncertainty, distraction, disruption, burden, risk, and expense of further litigation. Pursuant to the terms set forth below, this Stipulation (including the
exhibits) shall not in any event be construed as, or deemed to be evidence of, an admission or concession by the Individual Defendants with respect to any claim of fault, liability, wrongdoing, or damage or any defect in the defenses that Individual
Defendants have, or could have, asserted. Each Individual Defendant has further asserted, and continues to assert, that at all material times, the Individual Defendant acted in good faith and in a manner that she or he reasonably believed to be in
the best interests of Alphabet and its stockholders. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6
</P><DIV STYLE="line-height:3.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</DIV> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTICE OF PENDENCY AND

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHAT WILL HAPPEN IF THE SETTLEMENT IS APPROVED? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHAT CLAIMS WILL THE SETTLEMENT RELEASE? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">28. If the Settlement is approved, the Court will enter a Judgment. Pursuant to the Judgment, the Action will be dismissed in its entirety and
with prejudice and, upon the Effective Date of the Settlement,<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> the following releases will occur: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">29. <B>Release</B> <B>of</B> <B>Claims</B> <B>by</B> <B>Current</B> <B>Alphabet</B> <B>Stockholders</B>. Upon the Effective Date, the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs (acting on their own behalf and, in some cases, derivatively on behalf of Alphabet), Alphabet, and any Person acting derivatively on behalf of Alphabet shall be deemed to have, and by operation of
the Judgment shall have, fully, finally, and forever released, relinquished, discharged and dismissed with prejudice the Released Stockholder Claims which, as detailed in the Stipulation, means any and all claims, rights, demands, obligations,
controversies, debts, disputes, damages, losses, actions, causes of action, sums of money due, judgments, suits, amounts, matters, issues, liabilities, and charges of any kind or nature whatsoever (including, but not limited to, any claims for
interest, attorneys&#146; fees, expert or consulting fees, and any other costs, expenses, amounts, or liabilities whatsoever), and claims for relief of every nature and description whatsoever, whether in law or equity, including both known claims
and Unknown Claims (as defined in Paragraph I(aa) of the Stipulation), suspected or unsuspected, accrued or unaccrued, fixed or contingent, liquidated or unliquidated, matured or unmatured, foreseen or unforeseen, whether arising under federal or
state statutory or common law, or any other law, rule, or regulation, whether foreign or domestic, that Alphabet, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs derivatively on behalf of Alphabet, or any Alphabet stockholder
derivatively on behalf of Alphabet (i)&nbsp;asserted in any of the complaints filed in the Litigation, or (ii)&nbsp;could have asserted in any court, tribunal, forum, or proceeding, under the laws of any jurisdiction, arising out of, relating to, or
based upon the facts, allegations, events, disclosures, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-disclosures,</FONT> occurrences, representations, statements, matters, transactions, conduct, actions, failures to act, omissions, or circumstances that
were alleged or referred to in any of the complaints filed in the Litigation, regardless of the jurisdiction in which such facts, allegations, events, disclosures, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-disclosures,</FONT> occurrences,
representations, statements, matters, transactions, conduct, actions, failures to act, omissions, or circumstances were or could have been alleged or where such facts, allegations, events, disclosures,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-disclosures,</FONT> occurrences, representations, statements, matters, transactions, conduct, actions, failures to act, omissions, or circumstances had
impact.<SUP STYLE="font-size:75%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> In addition, Upon the Effective Date, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs (acting on their own behalf and, in some cases, derivatively on behalf of Alphabet),
Alphabet, and any Person acting derivatively on behalf of Alphabet, shall be forever barred and enjoined from asserting, commencing, instituting, or prosecuting any of the Released Stockholder Claims against any Released Defendant Persons,
regardless of the jurisdiction in which such claims were or could have been alleged or where the claims had impact. </P><DIV STYLE="line-height:8.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000;width:11%">&nbsp;</DIV>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">30. <B>Release</B> <B>of</B> <B>Claims</B> <B>by</B> <B>Defendants</B>. Upon the Effective

Alphabet&#146;s investor relations website at <U>https://abc.xyz/investor/</U> and on Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s website at <U>https://scott-scott.com/sdsettlements/alphabet-derivative-settlement/</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">HOW WILL THE STOCKHOLDERS&#146; ATTORNEYS BE PAID? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">33. Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel have not received any payment for their services in pursuing the claims asserted in the Action, nor have the
Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel been reimbursed for their litigation expenses. In light of benefits produced for Alphabet by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs and the Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel in connection with the
Settlement, Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel intend to seek approval from the Court for a Fee and Expense Award not to exceed $80,000,000. The Fee and Expense Award is separate from and in addition to the $500&nbsp;million spend amount. The Fee and

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
Expense Award, which includes litigation expenses and the Service Awards to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiffs, was negotiated with the assistance of and was the
result of a mediator&#146;s recommendation made by the mediator, the Hon. Layn R. Phillips (Ret.). Alphabet and the Individual Defendants agree not to oppose the requested Fee and Expense Award so long as it does not exceed $80,000,000. Alphabet
agrees that, to the extent available, it will cause insurance proceeds from the Defendants&#146; insurers to pay for the Fee and Expense Award in excess of any applicable self-insured retention. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT>
Plaintiffs further intend to seek approval from the Court for a Service Award for each <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT> Plaintiff not to exceed $50,000. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">34. The Court will determine the amount of the Fee and Expense Award for all Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel. Alphabet stockholders are not
personally liable for any such fees or expenses. Any fees and expenses approved by the Court will not diminish or have any impact on the $500&nbsp;million spend commitment by Alphabet pursuant to the Settlement (<I>see</I> Paragraph 22, above). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">WHEN AND WHERE WILL THE SETTLEMENT HEARING BE HELD? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">DO I HAVE THE RIGHT TO APPEAR AT THE SETTLEMENT HEARING? </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">35. The Court will consider the Settlement, as well as the Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s application for a Fee and Expense Award at the
Settlement Hearing. The Settlement Hearing will be held before The Honorable Rita F. Lin on September 30, 2025, at 1:30 p.m., both in person at the San Francisco Courthouse, Courtroom 15, 18th Floor, 450 Golden Gate Ave., San Francisco, CA 94102,
and online via the Court&#146;s public hearing Zoom Webinar&#151;accessible at <U>https://cand-uscourts.zoomgov.com/j1615482105?pwd=cTZiSVdXelllSXpjQ1p0Nm5HaXRYUT09</U>, Webinar ID: 161 548 2105 and password: 315725. At the Settlement Hearing, the
Court consider whether the Judgment, substantially in the form of Exhibit D to the Stipulation, should be entered: (a)&nbsp;approving the terms of the Settlement as fair, reasonable, and adequate; (b)&nbsp;dismissing with prejudice the Action
pursuant to the terms of this Stipulation; and (c)&nbsp;ruling upon Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s application for a Fee and Expense Award; and (d)&nbsp;to consider any other matters that may properly be brought before the Court in connection
with the Settlement. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">36. Any Alphabet stockholder who currently owns Alphabet stock may enter an appearance in the Action, at his, her,
or its own expense, individually or through counsel of his, her, or its own choice, by filing with the Clerk of the Court and delivering a notice of appearance to Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel and to Boris Feldman of Freshfields US LLP
(&#147;<B>Defendants&#146;</B> <B>Counsel</B>&#148;) at the addresses set forth in Paragraph 37 below, such that it is received no later than ten (10)&nbsp;calendar days prior to the Settlement Hearing, or as the Court may otherwise direct. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">37. Any Alphabet stockholder who currently owns Alphabet stock may file a written objection to the proposed Settlement and/or the
Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel&#146;s application for a Fee and Expense Award, and appear and show cause, if he, she, or it has any cause, why the proposed Settlement and/or the applications for such Fee and Expense Award should not be approved. All
Persons desiring to object are directed to file a written objection with the Clerk of the Court and serve (by hand, first-class mail, or express service) copies of such objection on Plaintiffs&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Lead</FONT>
Counsel and Defendants&#146; Counsel at the addresses set forth below such that they are <B><I>received</I></B> no later than September 20, 2025, which is ten (10)&nbsp;calendar days prior to the Settlement Hearing. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9

PROPOSED SETTLEMENT OF DERIVATIVE ACTION </P>

</DIV></Center>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">38. Any Alphabet stockholder who currently owns Alphabet stock and who wishes to be heard orally at the
Settlement Hearing may appear at the hearing, whether or not they have filed an objection. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">39. Any objections, filings, and other
submissions: (a)&nbsp;must state the name, address, and telephone number of the objector and, if represented by counsel, the name, address, and telephone number of his, her, or its counsel; (b)&nbsp;must be signed by the objector; (c)&nbsp;must
contain a specific, written statement of the objection(s) and the specific reason(s) for the objection(s), including any legal and evidentiary support the objector wishes to bring to the Court&#146;s attention, and if the objector has indicated that
he, she, or it intends to appear at the Settlement Hearing, the identity of any witnesses the objector may call to testify and any exhibits the objector intends to introduce into evidence at the hearing; and (d)&nbsp;must include documentation
sufficient to prove that the objector currently owns shares of Alphabet common stock and contain a statement that the objector continues to hold such shares as of the date of filing of the objection and will continue to hold those shares as of the
date of the Settlement Hearing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">40. Documentation establishing ownership of Alphabet common stock must consist of copies of monthly
brokerage account statements, or an authorized statement from the objector&#146;s broker containing the information found in an account statement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">41. You may file a written objection without having to appear at the Settlement Hearing. Any current Alphabet stockholder may also appear and
object at the Settlement Hearing with or without having submitted a written objection. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">42. You are not required to hire an attorney to
represent you in making written objections or in appearing at the Settlement Hearing. However, if you decide to hire an attorney, it will be at your own expense. If you file an objection in connection with or intend to appear at the Settlement
Hearing, your attorney should file a notice of appearance with the Court and serve it on Plaintiffs&#146; Lead Counsel and Defendants&#146; Counsel at the addresses set forth in Paragraph 37 above so that the notice is <B><I>received </I></B>on or
before September 20, 2025. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">43. Unless the Court orders otherwise, any Person who does not make his, her, or its
objection in the manner provided herein shall: (a)&nbsp;be deemed to have waived and forfeited his, her, or its right to object to any aspect of the proposed Settlement or Fee and Expense Awards and/or Service Awards; (b)&nbsp;be forever barred and
foreclosed from objecting to the fairness, reasonableness, or adequacy of the Settlement, the Judgment to be entered approving the Settlement, or the Fee and Expense Awards and/or Service Awards; and (c)&nbsp;be deemed to have waived and forever
barred and foreclosed from being heard, in this or any other proceeding, with respect to any matters concerning the Settlement or the contemplated and/or approved Fee and Expense Awards and Service Awards. </P>
